TITLE      -Tabulated Cross Sections For Hydrogen and Helium      O028900100003 
            Particles Produced by 62 and 29 MeV Protons on 120-Sn.O028900100004 
AUTHOR     (F.E.BERTRAND,R.W.PEELLE)                              O028900100005 
REFERENCE  (R,ORNL-4471,197007)                                   O028900100006 
           (J,PR/C,8,1045,1973) Combined Paper Where the Data For O028900100007 
           Some Targets were Collected.                           O028900100008 
INSTITUTE  (1USAORL)                                              O028900100009 
FACILITY   (ISOCY) Oak Ridge Isochronous Cyclotron.               O028900100010 
           (SPECM) Momentum Analyzed in a 153 Degree Magnet.      O028900100011 
INC-SPECT  .Monoenergetic 60.9 - 61.9 +/- 0.1 and 28.8 +/- 0.1 MeVO028900100012 
            Protons, Focused on the Target in a Spot of Approxi-  O028900100013 
            Mately 8 mm Diameter, with a Walk of +/- 0.4 Cm. The  O028900100014 
            Uncertainty in Number of Protons Striking the Target  O028900100015 
            Was +/- 1 %.                                          O028900100016 
METHOD     (EDE) The Secondary Particle Type was Identified with  O028900100017 
           (TOF) A Combination of Delta-E Versus E and Flight-    O028900100018 
            Time Versus E, Which Permitted Unambiguous            O028900100019 
           Identification from a Few MeV Up to 62 MeV. The        O028900100020 
           Low-Energy Cutoffs For the Different Particles were    O028900100021 
           ------------------------------------------------------ O028900100022 
           61.5 MeV                                               O028900100023 
                  Protons               1.8 MeV                   O028900100024 
                  Deuterons             4.6 MeV                   O028900100025 
                  Tritons               5.7 MeV                   O028900100026 
                  Helium-3             13.2 MeV                   O028900100027 
                  Alphas               11.0 MeV                   O028900100028 
             28.8 MeV                                             O028900100029 
                  Protons               1.9 MeV                   O028900100030 
                  Deuterons             4.6 MeV                   O028900100031 
                  Tritons               5.7 MeV                   O028900100032 
                  Helium-3             13.2 MeV                   O028900100033 
                  Alphas               11.0 MeV                   O028900100034 
           ------------------------------------------------------ O028900100035 
DETECTOR   (TELES,SOLST,GELI) A Solid State Three-Detector        O028900100036 
           Telescope, with Two Silicon Delta-E Detectors and a    O028900100037 
            Lithium-Drifted Germanium Detector Used For Total     O028900100038 
            Energy Absorption. The Delta-E Detectors had          O028900100039 
           Thicknesses of 100 and 500 Micrometers.                O028900100040 
           The  Telescope was Mounted in a Scattering Chamber withO028900100041 
           1.2 M Diameter.                                        O028900100042 
            The Total Resolution was Approximately 180 KeV For    O028900100043 
            Most of the Data. The Telescope was Shielded by       O028900100044 
           Tantalum  or Nickel Collimators.  For the 61.5 MeV RunsO028900100045 
            The Tantalum Collimator had a Thickness of 0.432 Cm   O028900100046 
            And an Area of 0.522 Cm2. The Two Nickel Collimators  O028900100047 
            Had a Thickness of 0.653 Cm and Areas of 0.183 and    O028900100048 
            0.265 Cm2, Respectively. For the 28.8 MeV Runs, a     O028900100049 
            0.013 Cm Thick Tantalum Collimator, with an Area of   O028900100050 
            O.522 Cm2, was Used. The Uncertainty in the           O028900100051 
           Collimator Areas was +/- 1.5 %.                        O028900100052 
           The Distance from                                      O028900100053 
            The Target to the Collimator was Around 46 Cm +/- 1%. O028900100054 
           The Collimators had a Misalignment at the Center of theO028900100055 
           Scattering Chamber of +/- 0.5 Cm.  The Precision of theO028900100056 
           Detector Angle was +/- 0.5 Degrees.                    O028900100057 
           The Zero Angle was Determined to +/- 0.5 Degrees.      O028900100058 
           The Angular Resolution was +/- 1.2 Degrees.            O028900100059 
SAMPLE     Tin Target, 4.85 +/- 0.05 Mg/Cm2 Thick, with a         O028900100060 
           Thickness Nonuniformity of +/- 1 %.  The Isotopic      O028900100061 
           Composition was 98.4 % 120-Sn, 0.5% 118-Sn, 0.4 %      O028900100062 
           119-Sn, 0.3 % 124-Sn and 0.4 % Other.                  O028900100063 
           The Sample had a Small Contaminant of Nickel and       O028900100064 
           Oxygen.   The Sample was Oriented with an Angular      O028900100065 
           Precision of +/- 0.5 Degrees.                          O028900100066 
CORRECTION .The Data were Corrected For                           O028900100067 
            1. Energy Loss of the Secondary Particles in the      O028900100068 
               Target,                                            O028900100069 
            2. Collimator Edge Penetration,                       O028900100070 
            3. Multiple Scattering of Particles in the First Two  O028900100071 
           Detectors, Which Made Them Miss the Total Absorption   O028900100072 
           Detector,                                              O028900100073 
            4. The Nickel Window Dead Layer of the Ge-Detector,   O028900100074 
               And,                                               O028900100075 
            5. Nuclear Reactions in the Ge-Detector.              O028900100076 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-S) Statistical Error in Data.                     O028900100077 
           (ERR-1) Systematic Error in Data, with Contributions   O028900100078 
            Such As                                               O028900100079 
            1. Uncertainty in Various Corrections  +/- 2 %.       O028900100080 
            2. Uncertainty in Number of Protons                   O028900100081 
               Striking the Target                 +/- 1 %.       O028900100082 
            3. Uncertainty in Dead Time            +/- 2 %.       O028900100083 
           (EN-ERR) Uncertainty of Beam Energy.                   O028900100084
